Please note that new updates will not apply to a server until it restarts.
PATCH 09/03/2020 (1):
  • Fixed the Montreal servers not having access to the blocked VPN database, which caused them to crash upon startup.
  • Increased the connection limit for all servers to 22, from 18.
  • Fixed beta-testers not being able to bypass the VPN blocker.
  • Fixed Arras Controller not being able to use its own commands.
  • Removed the message displayed when attempting to run Arras Controller's commands outside of the #bot-commands channel.
  • Reinstated ALL old changelogs which were previously removed. Hop on the nostalgia train with me.
PATCH 09/02/2020 (1): First of da month
  • Added an experimental VPN blocker due to heightened amounts of ban evasion by hunters and cheaters (huge shoutout to CX for this one!).
PATCH 08/29/2020 (1):
  • Performed some reworks to Arras Controller:
    • The new prefixes (previously posted in the polls channel) have been added, but the old prefixes will also be kept. Meaning you can use both sets.
    • The prefixhelp command has been updated to account for the new old and prefixes.
    • The help command has been tweaked such that the server's prefixes are displayed at the top of the command list.
    • Fixed some incorrect permissions.
    • When attempting to run commands outside of the #bot-commands channel, a message will now be displayed.
    • Renamed the devhelp command to advhelp.
    • Removed the reloadconfig command due to it not actually working.
PATCH 08/28/2020 (1): Some balance stuff
  • Rebuffed EK-3's health in Boss Rush back to 70% of what it used to be.
  • Buffed Hivemind Probe Bullet damage, penetration, and health by 10%.
  • Performed some reworks to Polygun to make it less buggy.
  • Fixed AI Bots being able to spawn as Kashmir (found by a lot of people).
  • Half N' Half now also branches from Napalm and Twin Gatling (suggested by black._.icce).
  • PS3_33 and PS3_33 Lite now also have the poison ability, to keep in-line with green shapes.
  • Performed some reworks to the Dropship boss:
    • Nerfed health by 33.333333%.
    • Lowered the max Minion count to 8, from 10.
    • Fixed the Auto Turrets having faster reload than intended.
    • Fixed the Auto Turret AI being nonexistent.
ANNOUNCEMENT 08/25/2020: Update on "cursor lag"
  • The brand new Chrome update (Chrome 85) has fixed the cursor lagging issue. If you are a Chrome user, update your browsers now. Whether this has been fixed in other Chromium browsers is currently unknown.

ANNOUNCEMENT 08/21/2020: Addressing "cursor lag"
  • As of recently, this is an issue that has appeared in both Arras and Woomy Arras, on Chromium-based browsers. Until a fix can be attained, some temporary fixes include:
    • Using the Firefox browser (clear cache first).
    • Opening a new window and opening the F12 (or Ctrl+Shift+I) menu on the new window.
    • Using the Google Chrome Canary browser (found by [O] Blood).
PATCH 08/21/2020 (2): Bugs are gross
  • For those experiencing issues joining any of the servers, clear your cache and cookies.
  • Fixed bosses sometimes not spawning.
  • Fixed some bosses having very weak and/or broken stats.
PATCH 08/21/2020 (1): Boss rush's grand opening
  • This game mode is brand new; bugs and balance issues will likely arise. Please report any bugs or balance issues in our Discord server.
  • Added Boss Rush as a replacement game mode for 4TDM Mothership.
  • The time limit tanks have to win the game is 30 minutes.

PATCH 06/01/2020 (1): NEW GAMEMODES?!
  • Addressing the new servers, they might be buggy. Please continue to report any bugs that you find.
  • Added 2TDM:
    • A mode with 2 teams, pretty self-explanatory.
    • Team bases are horizontal across the whole left and right side of the map.
  • Added Portal Domination:
    • The map is split into 4, with portals at the center of each split area.
    • Dominators are located at the corners.
    • Capture 4 Dominators to win the game.
    • Helicopter-based tanks can now fly over the map dividers, but also will fly above portals and take damage (partially due to a bug found by DUO).
  • Added 4TDM Mothership:
    • 4 teams, 4 Motherships. Each of them spawn at the corners of the map.
    • The team with the last Mothership remaining wins the game.
  • Added 4TDM Maze:
    • 4TDM just got interesting. Now there's maze walls you need to navigate through.
    • The idea for TDM Maze is from Oblivion de Plain.
  • Shoutout to Feixu for helping me fix a mockups issue with these servers.
  • Fixed Dropship's Assassin barrel shooting traps (found by PS3_33).
  • Added a "Loading entity mockups..." message that appears when mockups haven't fully loaded.

    • Bot FoV is rebuffed (mostly) back to its previous level.

PATCH 03/23/2020 (1): Mothership
  • We've added yet another new game mode: Mothership!
  • Here are the basics:
    • There are two teams, so there are two Motherships that spawn in the corners of the map.
    • Each Mothership has a name color which matches their team.
    • Unlike Diep and main Arras Mothership, you can press H to control your team's Mothership.
    • You can choose what build your team's Mothership will use, so choose it wisely.
    • Kill the opposing team's Mothership to win the game.
  • Shoutout to Oblivion Plain for offering us the game mode's code (originally made by CX).
  • Since this is a brand new game mode, bugs aren't outside of the picture. If you find some, report them to us so we may fix them.

PATCH 03/07/2020 (3): The Second Coming
  • We're proud to announce that we're releasing a new server with a new game mode: 2 Team Domination!
  • To keep it simple, the rules of Domination are simple:
    • 5 different Dominators are scattered around the map, each with its own challenging characteristics.
    • These Dominators spawn yellow, and will attack any tank. Yellow Dominators are considered "contested".
    • If you kill one, you capture it into your team.
    • If the opposing team kills your Dominator, it becomes "contested" again.
    • Capture 4 Dominators, and you win the game! The arena closes and it all resets.
  • To get to the new server, hover your mouse over the server name (above the name text box), scroll down, and select "2 Team Domination".
  • Arras Controller also works with the new server. The command prefix for it is _ instead of +.

    • Toggled by pressing the U key.
    • Use the left and right arrow keys to cycle through the class tree.

PATCH 11/23/2018 (5)
  • NOTE: These changes will take affect after the server restarts!
  • The following changes have been made to the Arras Controller bot:
    • Added a +setgodmode command, which enables/disables god mode for a specified user (meaning that user can't die if it's enabled).
    • Added a +setpassive command, which enables/disables passive mode for a specified user (meaning that user can't harm or be harmed if it's enabled).
    • If you ping the bot, it will send a pingsock.

PATCH 09/29/2018 (2)
  • Added the experimental Grower branch, ideas by [RR] Rodrigo and kot32.
  • NOTE: They may not be balanced, so please give balance suggestions for each tank.
  • All stats for Mini Grower go as follows:
    • Reload nerfed by half.
    • Bullets stop moving after about 3 seconds.
    • Bullets disappear after about 3 seconds.
    • Bullet size increases by about 1/3rd per second.
    • Bullet damage increases by about 1/2nd per second.
    • Bullet penetration increases by about 1/5th per second.
  • Each tier upgrade increases bullet reload speed and bullet deceleration speed.
  • However, each tier upgrade also makes bullet size, penetration, and damage per second increase faster.
  • The branch currently consists of Mini Grower, Grower, Mega Grower, and Giga Grower.

  • So if you want the normal, rounded edges that arras offers, make sure that option is not checked.

PATCH 04/29/2018 (2)
  • Your score (above your level bar) now displays exact value instead of a rounded value.
  • Changed up some of the browser console commands:
  • The command color() is now setColor().
  • The commands broadcast() and setColor() no longer require a password, but rather a beta tester token.
  • Added the setSkill() command: It sets how many skill points you have (also requires a beta tester token).
  • Usage for broadcast() is broadcast("message").
  • Usage for setColor() is setColor(colorID). The colorID can be anything from 0-28.
  • Usage for setSkill() is setSkill(skillAmount). The skillAmount can be anywhere from 0-90.
  • Replaced ALL beta tester tokens with new ones due to people complaining about not having beta tester.
